   QUATERNIZATION; NARROW MOLECULAR WEIGHT DISTRIBUTION; INTRINSIC
   VISCOSITY; EXPANSION FACTOR
ID EXCLUDED-VOLUME; "POLY(4-VINYLBENZYLTRIMETHYLAMMONIUM CHLORIDE);
   AQUEOUS-SOLUTION; POLYELECTROLYTE
AB Anionically polymerized poly(2-vinylpyridine) was sucessfully quaternized with dimethyl sulfate in dimethlformamide at room temperature without degradation and coloring to prepare poly(N-methyl-2-vinylpyridinum chloride) (PMVP-C1) with narrow molecular weight distributions.  It was found that the intrinsic viscosity of PMVP-Cl in NaCl solutions agrees with the Stockmayer-Fixman equation except for high molecular weight samples at low ionic strengths, and the cubic of the expansion factor due to electrostatic repulsion obtained from intrinsic viscosity alpha-3-n is expressed as a linear function of (M/C(s))1/2 as reported for poly(sodium acrylate).
